<p class="has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-bf3a46da421bead2b5058b424acb7fb6" style="margin-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);margin-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);font-size:18px">Honest travel guides, practical tips, <br>and plenty of awkward stories<br></p>

<p class=""></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">All right, here&#8217;s the deal</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I’m Natalie, an introverted digital nomad slow traveling the U.S. with my dog, Elgie. Over the course of four years, we&#8217;ve lived in 11 states and visited many others.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I started Outsider Odyssey for 3 reasons–</p>



<div class="wp-block-group"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li class="">To inspire you to travel the United States. It’s beautiful!</li>



<li class="">To make the digital nomad lifestyle, and travel in general, feel more accessible and achievable. If I, an awkward, neurodivergent introvert with a dog, can do it, so can you!</li>



<li class="">To show that the above can -and should- be done with a sense of humor. Because if you can’t laugh at your own cringy stories, what&#8217;s the point? And besides, more than anything else, travel should be fun!</li>
</ol>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">

</div>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Meet Elgie</h3>



<p class="">Elgie, a.k.a. L.G. (Little Guy), is a 14-year-old lab/corgi mix who loves swimming, chasing balls, and hiking with his mommy. He barks at every noise he hears outside and hasn&#8217;t met a cat or a sprinkler he didn&#8217;t like. He loves car rides and is used to his mom packing him all over creation.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">For People Tired of Trying So Hard</h2>

	<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://outsiderodyssey.com/how-to-become-a-digital-nomad-in-the-u-s/" rel="bookmark">How to Become a Digital Nomad in the U.S. (Step-by-Step Guide)</a></h2>	<div class="entry-meta entry-meta-divider-dot">

	<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://outsiderodyssey.com/avoiding-digital-nomad-burnout/" rel="bookmark">When Even Travel Feels Like Work: Avoiding Digital Nomad Burnout</a></h2>	<div class="entry-meta entry-meta-divider-dot">
